         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/NullPointerException.html">NullPointerException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if <code>target</code> or <code>replacement</code> is <code>null</code>.</td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <a name="replace(char, char)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">replace</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> replace (char oldChar, 
                char newChar)</pre> 
      <p>Returns a string resulting from replacing all occurrences of <code>oldChar</code> in this string with <code>newChar</code>. </p>
      <p> If the character <code>oldChar</code> does not occur in the character sequence represented by this <code>String</code> object, then a reference to this <code>String</code> object is returned. Otherwise, a <code>String</code> object is returned that represents a character sequence identical to the character sequence represented by this <code>String</code> object, except that every occurrence of <code>oldChar</code> is replaced by an occurrence of <code>newChar</code>. </p>
      <p> Examples: </p>
      <blockquote>
       <pre>
 "mesquite in your cellar".replace('e', 'o')
         returns "mosquito in your collar"
 "the war of baronets".replace('r', 'y')
         returns "the way of bayonets"
 "sparring with a purple porpoise".replace('p', 't')
         returns "starring with a turtle tortoise"
 "JonL".replace('q', 'x') returns "JonL" (no change)
 </pre>
      </blockquote>
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>oldChar</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>char</code>: the old character.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>newChar</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>char</code>: the new character.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">a string derived from this string by replacing every occurrence of <code>oldChar</code> with <code>newChar</code>. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <a name="replaceAll(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">replaceAll</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> replaceAll (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> regex, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> replacement)</pre> 
      <p>Replaces each substring of this string that matches the given <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html#sum">regular expression</a> with the given replacement. </p>
      <p> An invocation of this method of the form <i>str</i><code>.replaceAll(</code><i>regex</i><code>,</code> <i>repl</i><code>)</code> yields exactly the same result as the expression </p>
      <blockquote> 
       <code> <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html">Pattern</a></code>.<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html#compile(java.lang.String)">compile</a></code>(<i>regex</i>).<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html#matcher(java.lang.CharSequence)">matcher</a></code>(<i>str</i>).<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Matcher.html#replaceAll(java.lang.String)">replaceAll</a></code>(<i>repl</i>) </code> 
      </blockquote> 
      <p> Note that backslashes (<code>\</code>) and dollar signs (<code>$</code>) in the replacement string may cause the results to be different than if it were being treated as a literal replacement string; see <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Matcher.html#replaceAll(java.lang.String)">Matcher.replaceAll</a></code>. Use <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Matcher.html#quoteReplacement(java.lang.String)">quoteReplacement(String)</a></code> to suppress the special meaning of these characters, if desired.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>regex</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: the regular expression to which this string is to be matched<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>replacement</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: the string to be substituted for each match<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">The resulting <code>String</code><p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/PatternSyntaxException.html">PatternSyntaxException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if the regular expression's syntax is invalid</td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html">Pattern</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <a name="replaceFirst(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">replaceFirst</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> replaceFirst (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> regex, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> replacement)</pre> 
      <p>Replaces the first substring of this string that matches the given <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html#sum">regular expression</a> with the given replacement. </p>
      <p> An invocation of this method of the form <i>str</i><code>.replaceFirst(</code><i>regex</i><code>,</code> <i>repl</i><code>)</code> yields exactly the same result as the expression </p>
      <blockquote> 
       <code> <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html">Pattern</a></code>.<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html#compile(java.lang.String)">compile</a></code>(<i>regex</i>).<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html#matcher(java.lang.CharSequence)">matcher</a></code>(<i>str</i>).<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Matcher.html#replaceFirst(java.lang.String)">replaceFirst</a></code>(<i>repl</i>) </code> 
      </blockquote> 
      <p> Note that backslashes (<code>\</code>) and dollar signs (<code>$</code>) in the replacement string may cause the results to be different than if it were being treated as a literal replacement string; see <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Matcher.html#replaceFirst(java.lang.String)">replaceFirst(String)</a></code>. Use <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Matcher.html#quoteReplacement(java.lang.String)">quoteReplacement(String)</a></code> to suppress the special meaning of these characters, if desired.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>regex</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: the regular expression to which this string is to be matched<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>replacement</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: the string to be substituted for the first match<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">The resulting <code>String</code><p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/PatternSyntaxException.html">PatternSyntaxException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if the regular expression's syntax is invalid</td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html">Pattern</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <a name="split(java.lang.String, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">split</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String[]</a> split (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> regex, 
                int limit)</pre> 
      <p>Splits this string around matches of the given <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html#sum">regular expression</a>. </p>
      <p> The array returned by this method contains each substring of this string that is terminated by another substring that matches the given expression or is terminated by the end of the string. The substrings in the array are in the order in which they occur in this string. If the expression does not match any part of the input then the resulting array has just one element, namely this string. </p>
      <p> When there is a positive-width match at the beginning of this string then an empty leading substring is included at the beginning of the resulting array. A zero-width match at the beginning however never produces such empty leading substring. </p>
      <p> The <code>limit</code> parameter controls the number of times the pattern is applied and therefore affects the length of the resulting array. If the limit <i>n</i> is greater than zero then the pattern will be applied at most <i>n</i>&nbsp;-&nbsp;1 times, the array's length will be no greater than <i>n</i>, and the array's last entry will contain all input beyond the last matched delimiter. If <i>n</i> is non-positive then the pattern will be applied as many times as possible and the array can have any length. If <i>n</i> is zero then the pattern will be applied as many times as possible, the array can have any length, and trailing empty strings will be discarded. </p>
      <p> The string <code>"boo:and:foo"</code>, for example, yields the following results with these parameters: </p>
      <blockquote>
       <table cellpadding="1" cellspacing="0" summary="Split example showing regex, limit, and result"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr> 
          <th>Regex</th> 
          <th>Limit</th> 
          <th>Result</th> 
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td align="center">:</td> 
          <td align="center">2</td> 
          <td><code>{ "boo", "and:foo" }</code></td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td align="center">:</td> 
          <td align="center">5</td> 
          <td><code>{ "boo", "and", "foo" }</code></td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td align="center">:</td> 
          <td align="center">-2</td> 
          <td><code>{ "boo", "and", "foo" }</code></td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td align="center">o</td> 
          <td align="center">5</td> 
          <td><code>{ "b", "", ":and:f", "", "" }</code></td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td align="center">o</td> 
          <td align="center">-2</td> 
          <td><code>{ "b", "", ":and:f", "", "" }</code></td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td align="center">o</td> 
          <td align="center">0</td> 
          <td><code>{ "b", "", ":and:f" }</code></td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table>
      </blockquote> 
      <p> An invocation of this method of the form <i>str.</i><code>split(</code><i>regex</i><code>,</code>&nbsp;<i>n</i><code>)</code> yields the same result as the expression </p>
      <blockquote> 
       <code> <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html">Pattern</a></code>.<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html#compile(java.lang.String)">compile</a></code>(<i>regex</i>).<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html#split(java.lang.CharSequence, int)">split</a></code>(<i>str</i>,&nbsp;<i>n</i>) </code> 
      </blockquote>
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>regex</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: the delimiting regular expression<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>limit</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: the result threshold, as described above<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String[]</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">the array of strings computed by splitting this string around matches of the given regular expression<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/PatternSyntaxException.html">PatternSyntaxException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if the regular expression's syntax is invalid</td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/regex/Pattern.html">Pattern</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <a name="split(java.lang.String)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">split</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in

      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String[]</a> split (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> regex)</pre>

     <a name="substring(int, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">substring</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> substring (int beginIndex, 
                int endIndex)</pre> 
      <p>Returns a string that is a substring of this string. The substring begins at the specified <code>beginIndex</code> and extends to the character at index <code>endIndex - 1</code>. Thus the length of the substring is <code>endIndex-beginIndex</code>. </p>
      <p> Examples: </p>
      <blockquote>
       <pre>
 "hamburger".substring(4, 8) returns "urge"
 "smiles".substring(1, 5) returns "mile"
 </pre>
      </blockquote>

        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>endIndex</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: the ending index, exclusive.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

        </tr>

        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>

         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/IndexOutOfBoundsException.html">IndexOutOfBoundsException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if the <code>beginIndex</code> is negative, or <code>endIndex</code> is larger than the length of this <code>String</code> object, or <code>beginIndex</code> is larger than <code>endIndex</code>. </td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

     <a name="toLowerCase()"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">toLowerCase</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> toLowerCase ()</pre> 
      <p>Converts all of the characters in this <code>String</code> to lower case using the rules of the default locale. This is equivalent to calling <code>toLowerCase(Locale.getDefault())</code>. </p>
      <p> <b>Note:</b> This method is locale sensitive, and may produce unexpected results if used for strings that are intended to be interpreted locale independently. Examples are programming language identifiers, protocol keys, and HTML tags. For instance, <code>"TITLE".toLowerCase()</code> in a Turkish locale returns <code>"t\u0131tle"</code>, where '\u0131' is the LATIN SMALL LETTER DOTLESS I character. To obtain correct results for locale insensitive strings, use <code>toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)</code>. </p>
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">the <code>String</code>, converted to lowercase.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div>

      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> toLowerCase (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/Locale.html">Locale</a> locale)</pre> 
      <p>Converts all of the characters in this <code>String</code> to lower case using the rules of the given <code>Locale</code>. Case mapping is based on the Unicode Standard version specified by the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/Character.html">Character</a></code> class. Since case mappings are not always 1:1 char mappings, the resulting <code>String</code> may be a different length than the original <code>String</code>. </p>

         <td>tr (Turkish)</td>

         <td>capital letter I -&gt; small letter dotless i </td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr>

         <td>lowercased all chars in String</td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td>(all)</td> 
         <td><img src="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/doc-files/capiota.gif" alt="capiota"><img src="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/doc-files/capchi.gif" alt="capchi"> <img src="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/doc-files/captheta.gif" alt="captheta"><img src="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/doc-files/capupsil.gif" alt="capupsil"> <img src="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/doc-files/capsigma.gif" alt="capsigma"></td> 
         <td><img src="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/doc-files/iota.gif" alt="iota"><img src="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/doc-files/chi.gif" alt="chi"> <img src="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/doc-files/theta.gif" alt="theta"><img src="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/doc-files/upsilon.gif" alt="upsilon"> <img src="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/doc-files/sigma1.gif" alt="sigma"></td>

     <a name="toUpperCase()"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">toUpperCase</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> toUpperCase ()</pre> 
      <p>Converts all of the characters in this <code>String</code> to upper case using the rules of the default locale. This method is equivalent to <code>toUpperCase(Locale.getDefault())</code>. </p>
      <p> <b>Note:</b> This method is locale sensitive, and may produce unexpected results if used for strings that are intended to be interpreted locale independently. Examples are programming language identifiers, protocol keys, and HTML tags. For instance, <code>"title".toUpperCase()</code> in a Turkish locale returns <code>"T\u0130TLE"</code>, where '\u0130' is the LATIN CAPITAL LETTER I WITH DOT ABOVE character. To obtain correct results for locale insensitive strings, use <code>toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT)</code>. </p>
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">the <code>String</code>, converted to uppercase.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html#toUpperCase(java.util.Locale)">toUpperCase(Locale)</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <a name="trim()"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">trim</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> trim ()</pre> 
      <p>Returns a string whose value is this string, with any leading and trailing whitespace removed. </p>
      <p> If this <code>String</code> object represents an empty character sequence, or the first and last characters of character sequence represented by this <code>String</code> object both have codes greater than <code>'\u0020'</code> (the space character), then a reference to this <code>String</code> object is returned. </p>
      <p> Otherwise, if there is no character with a code greater than <code>'\u0020'</code> in the string, then a <code>String</code> object representing an empty string is returned. </p>
      <p> Otherwise, let <i>k</i> be the index of the first character in the string whose code is greater than <code>'\u0020'</code>, and let <i>m</i> be the index of the last character in the string whose code is greater than <code>'\u0020'</code>. A <code>String</code> object is returned, representing the substring of this string that begins with the character at index <i>k</i> and ends with the character at index <i>m</i>-that is, the result of <code>this.substring(k, m + 1)</code>. </p>
      <p> This method may be used to trim whitespace (as defined above) from the beginning and end of a string.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">A string whose value is this string, with any leading and trailing white space removed, or this string if it has no leading or trailing white space. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div>

     <a name="valueOf(char[], int, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">valueOf</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> valueOf (char[] data, 
                int offset, 
                int count)</pre> 
      <p>Returns the string representation of a specific subarray of the <code>char</code> array argument. </p>
      <p> The <code>offset</code> argument is the index of the first character of the subarray. The <code>count</code> argument specifies the length of the subarray. The contents of the subarray are copied; subsequent modification of the character array does not affect the returned string.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>data</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>char</code>: the character array.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>offset</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: initial offset of the subarray.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>count</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: length of the subarray.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">a <code>String</code> that contains the characters of the specified subarray of the character array.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/IndexOutOfBoundsException.html">IndexOutOfBoundsException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if <code>offset</code> is negative, or <code>count</code> is negative, or <code>offset+count</code> is larger than <code>data.length</code>. </td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div>

        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">a string representation of the <code>long</code> argument.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/Long.html#toString(long)">toString(long)</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <a name="valueOf(java.lang.Object)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">valueOf</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> valueOf (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/Object.html">Object</a> obj)</pre> 
      <p>Returns the string representation of the <code>Object</code> argument.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>obj</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>Object</code>: an <code>Object</code>.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if the argument is <code>null</code>, then a string equal to <code>"null"</code>; otherwise, the value of <code>obj.toString()</code> is returned.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/Object.html#toString()">toString()</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <a name="valueOf(char[])"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">valueOf</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> valueOf (char[] data)</pre> 
      <p>Returns the string representation of the <code>char</code> array argument. The contents of the character array are copied; subsequent modification of the character array does not affect the returned string.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>data</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>char</code>: the character array.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">a <code>String</code> that contains the characters of the character array. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <!-- ========= METHOD DETAIL ======== --> 
     <!-- ========= END OF CLASS DATA ========= --> 
    </div>

      if (lang === 'en') { return; }

    })(getLangPref())
